msg:Xizi Hotel Review:
As an old state guesthouse, Xizi Hotel's environment and greenery are beyond reproach, especially such a large area of ‚Äã‚Äãgreenery, which is lush and green. Upgraded to a suite, with a balcony, a Dyson hair dryer in the bathroom, a Salvatore Ferragamo toiletries set, a lot of bottled water, and a bucket of Hupao water. The hardware facilities are well maintained. Building No. 3 has a dedicated housekeeper. Due to the inconvenience of traveling to the scenic spot on weekends, Manager Yang in the lobby also arranged a vehicle to send us to Liuyingli for tea. The room attendants would also take the initiative to greet "good morning" when they met in the corridor.
Next, let's talk about the software. From the front desk reception, to the battery car driver, to the waiter in the breakfast restaurant, and even the female housekeeper in Building No. 3, to be honest, the service is really not up to this level of standard, especially the waiter in the restaurant, who doesn't even have the most basic courtesy that an ordinary restaurant should have. He took away the plates that the guests were still eating, and put the chopsticks directly on the table. The table was not cleaned and the placemat was directly placed. He started sweeping the floor next to our table before nine o'clock, etc., etc., too lacking professional training.
Maybe the state guesthouse is still in the state of "the emperor's daughter has no trouble finding a husband". At least the service of foreign chain hotels of the same level will not be bad.
Xizi Hotel, Wangzhuang, has beautiful scenery and the restaurant environment is also beautiful. You can see the West Lake, which is pleasing to the eye. All five stars are given to the environment and the beautiful scenery of the West Lake.

msg:After studying the strategy, I finally chose Xizi Hotel, which was a good experience.
As soon as I entered the hotel gate, I could already appreciate the difference between the crowds and the private forest garden, the quiet environment, and the warm greetings. The accommodation room is spacious and bright, the room structure is square and very a**ospheric, and the facilities are complete, even mosquito repellent is considered. You can make a small pot of tea in the room and drink it by yourself. This is probably the tradition of Wangzhuang.
Walking in the manor at different times has different feelings. The quietness of the mountains on the other side of the lake in the early morning, the noise across the lake in the afternoon, and the gorgeous lights of Leifeng Pagoda in the evening. It saves the trip around the lake, which is very suitable for taking the elderly out.
It is worth mentioning that the free travel photography met Mr. Kongkong, who is nice and humorous. His photography and photo editing skills are excellent, and he can easily take a big picture.
Overall, this trip to Xizi Hotel is worth the money.

It faces the lake to the east, is adjacent to the famous ancient temple Jingci to the south, and is adjacent to "Sudi" Famous scenery such as "Three Ponds Mirroring the Moon" and "Singing Orioles in the Willow Waves" are across the lake. msg:Zhejiang Xizi Hotel Wangzhuang is a garden-style hotel located at the foot of the "Leifeng Sunset" mountain and on the edge of the West Lake. It faces the lake on three sides and has beautiful scenery. It is adjacent to the famous ancient temple Jingci in the south. It faces famous scenery such as "Spring Dawn on Su Causeway", "Three Ponds Reflecting the Moon", "Singing the Orioles in the Waves in the Willows" and other famous scenery across the lake. It can also overlook the north and south peaks, Santai Mountain, Baochu Tower, Chenghuang Pavilion, etc.; you have a panoramic view of the lakes and mountains, especially the sunrise in the morning and the sunset in the evening are very stunning and shocking; the hotel has a beautiful environment, elegant and beautiful, quiet and quiet, with the Xizhao Mountain in the background and the Ripples built on the south bank of the West Lake. Every step in the garden makes people dizzy and forget to leave. Visitors take a walk along the unique lake shoreline that is more than one kilometer long. The breeze is gentle, the lake water is slightly rippled, pink peach blossoms are swaying, and cherry blossoms or begonia flowers are falling gracefully. It is pleasant. Incomparable.
The hotel service is first-class, the room facilities are complete, and the hotel is clean and tidy. The hotel staff have a strong sense of service and are kind, enthusiastic and thoughtful. In particular, Yu Liqian, the housekeeper in Building 2, took the initiative to connect with us and help us solve various problems we encountered during check-in and during our stay. She offered fruits and pastries as gifts, often asked us what we needed, and helped us carry all the bulky things when we checked out. The luggage was put in the taxi; the waiter, Master Le, was enthusiastic and kind. He always tidied the room in time according to our requirements, distributed a large amount of drinking water, often asked us what we needed, and organized staff to move and adjust the mattress on the day we checked in. , so that we could have a better bed rest; the young men at the concierge who drove a battery car and were responsible for picking up and dropping off in the park responded to all requests and answered all questions, and their performance was very eye-catching! The hotel's buffet breakfast has many varieties, is of good quality, and is very rich. It has the flavor of Hangzhou's local snacks and the characteristics of a state hotel. It is a delicacy.
In March, the most beautiful West Lake and the most beautiful Xizi Hotel!

msg:View the beautiful scenery of West Lake and stay at Xizi Hotel.
Xizi Hotel, Hangzhou, Zhejiang, also known as Wangzhuang, was originally Wang Yutai Tea House (founded in 1927). It is located on the south bank of West Lake in Hangzhou, adjacent to the Leifeng Pagoda, a historic site. It is bordered by the lake on three sides, surrounded by mountains and rivers, and enjoys the unique scenery of West Lake.
We checked in on November 27th. At 4 pm that day, we participated in the activity organized by the hotel to re-walk the state guest route of the 19th Asian Games in Hangzhou. The tour guide enthusiastically led our group of tourists to re-walk the state guest route of the Asian Games. Details Introduced the situation of the hotel, introduced the reception scene of the Asian Games in the hotel and the welcome banquet venue, guided the tour of the "Qiantang Tide" tableware used for the Asian Games banquet, and introduced the welcome dinner and tableware "West Lake Charm" for the G20 Hangzhou Summit held in Hangzhou Xizi Hotel that year ", guided a tour of the scene where Chairman Mao Zedong stayed at the Xizi Hotel and the preserved tableware. The tour guide also enthusiastically introduced the history of Wangzhuang and its historical buildings, the tea garden in the hotel and the annual tea-picking season activities of the hotel. The tour guide also introduced the traffic situation around the West Lake in Hangzhou, introduced the architecture of Hu Xueyan's former residence in Hangzhou, and patiently answered various questions from tourists. It is worth expressing my gratitude here for her enthusiastic and generous tour.
The experience of staying at Xizi Hotel is very good. The front desk staff warmly welcomes and introduces us and guides us to check in. There is an evening service after checking into the room. The room staff is enthusiastic about their work.
The hotel has a variety of breakfast options, and the breakfast room where you have breakfast has a nice view. You can enjoy the scenery while having breakfast.
Since Xizi Hotel is located near the beautiful West Lake, it is really beautiful to walk on the trail of Xizi Hotel and watch the scenery of the West Lake and the autumn trees of the hotel.

We stayed in the State Guesthouse and Xizi Hotel for one night each. Although it is a bit troublesome to change hotels, we still want to experience the difference between these two hotels.

The Xizi Hotel was full on the day of check-in, and the hotel also hosted a wedding banquet, which was very crowded.

Compared with the State Guesthouse, Xizi Hotel has a more a**ospheric scenery. It is located by the West Lake and at the foot of Leifeng Tower. It's a pity that the turf in front of Building No. 1 is under repair, otherwise it would be an excellent location for taking pictures.

The service of Xizi Hotel is slightly worse than that of the State Guesthouse. There is no turndown service and no guardrail for children.

The room facilities are hard to describe, it is really a hotel... The price of 2,000+, at most, the facilities of a three-star hotel. The curtains can't be closed, the light is transparent, and I wake up early in the morning; the shower is hot and cold, there is no bathtub, and the bathroom is pitifully small.

ps. The hotel can make reservations for West Lake cruises, only for in-house guests, the trip takes about an hour, and the price is reasonable.
